NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Companies Act, 1956
Member’s (or Creditors’) Voluntary Winding Up
Notice of Appointment of Liquidator pursuant to Section 516
Name of the Company

:

M/s. A.S. Trucking Private Limited

Nature of Business

:

Business of all Freight Services such as
Custom House Agents and other Transport Services

Address of Registered Office

:

Members in Extraordinary General Meeting Held on

Chennai,

A. SATYA DEVI,
Liquidator.

A.S. TRUCKING PRIVATE LIMITED
Navin’s Presidium, 8th Floor, B-Block, 173 Nelson Manickam Road
Aminjikarai, Chennai - 600 029 .
Pursuant to section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at an Extraordinary
General Meeting of the Company held on 30-06-2016 the following Special Resolution was passed
unanimously to voluntarily wind up M/s. A. S. Trucking Private Limited.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 29-06-2016 made by the Board of
Directors of the Company under section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company
would be able to pay its debts in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof,
the company, having its Registered Office at Navin’s Presidium, 8th Floor, B-Block, 173 Nelson Manickam
Road, Aminjikarai, Chennai - 600 029, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
8th July 2016.

IQBAL RAHMAN,
Director.

July 13, 2016]
